35:1339:70659:27:69:90:522:212:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:higher  than  those  submitted  by  agents  with  identical  risk  preference  in  the  baseline,  no-
35:1340:70761:69:7:234:237:143:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:                                                 
35:1341:70809:7:16:90:524:136:42:g_d0_f3:100:g_d0_f3:18 We categorize the level of CARA risk preference for the agent based upon estimates provided on p. 1649 
35:1342:70915:16:12:90:528:120:100:g_d0_f3:100:g_d0_f3:of    Holt  and  Laury  (2002).    Risk-averse  agents  are  those  who  select  more  than  4  of  the  “safe”  choices.    
35:1343:71040:12:11:90:525:108:100:g_d0_f3:100:g_d0_f3:Slightly risk averse agents are those who select between 5 and 7 “safe” choices.  Highly risk averse agents 
35:1344:71148:11:12:90:526:97:100:g_d0_f3:100:g_d0_f3:are  those  who  select  more  than  7  “safe”  choices  in  the  Holt  and  Laury  experiment.    These  categories  
35:1345:71266:12:11:90:524:85:100:g_d0_f3:100:g_d0_f3:correspond to a CARA value of 0.1 ≤ CARA ≤ 0.49 for slightly risk averse agents and 0.5 ≤ CARA ≤ ∞ for 
35:1346:71368:11:36:90:194:74:100:g_d0_f3:100:g_d0_f3:highly risk averse agents. 
36:1347:71395:36:0:295:318:38:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:-35- 
36:1348:71400:0:27:89:525:708:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:resale treatment.  Finally, these differences are an increasing function for signals less than 
36:1349:71495:27:28:89:377:681:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:$20, and a decreasing function for signals above this range. 
36:1350:71556:28:27:125:525:653:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: To examine these differences in a statistical model, we estimate a random effects 
36:1351:71638:27:28:89:525:626:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:regression model where the absolute difference:  |risk neutral predicted bid – actual bid| is 
36:1352:71732:28:28:89:525:598:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:regressed on treatment dummy variables, individual risk preference, and an interaction of 
36:1353:71822:28:27:89:470:570:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:individual risk preference and signals.  This estimation leads to the next result: 
36:1354:71905:27:14:107:522:543:144:g_d0_f5:144:g_d0_f5:Result  5:  Risk-averse  bidders  submit  bids  that  differ  more  from  the  theoretical  risk-
36:1355:72002:14:14:107:525:529:144:g_d0_f5:144:g_d0_f5:neutral  benchmarks  than  do  bids  of  risk-neutral  (loving)  agents,  with  the  difference  
36:1356:72099:14:14:107:367:515:144:g_d0_f5:144:g_d0_f5:increasing in the level of observed risk aversion.         
36:1357:72158:14:13:107:110:501:144:g_d0_f5:144:g_d0_f5: 
36:1358:72158:13:28:89:525:488:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:Support for Result 5 can be found in Table 7.  For example, in column A, rows 4 and 7 of 
36:1359:72247:28:28:89:526:460:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:the  table,  we  see  that  highly  risk  averse  agents  (denoted  HRA  in  Table  7)  submit  bids  
36:1360:72349:28:27:89:526:432:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:that,  on  average,  diverge  from  an  associated  risk-neutral  prediction  by  $5.52,  with  this  
36:1361:72451:27:28:89:525:405:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:difference decreasing by $0.18 for a dollar increase in signal.  Both of these differences 
36:1362:72542:28:27:89:525:377:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:are  significant  at  the  p  <  0.05  level.    These  differences  decrease  to  2.88  and  0.09  when  
36:1363:72648:27:28:89:526:350:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:slightly  risk  averse  agents  (denoted  SRA  in  the  table)  are  considered.    As  a  robustness  
36:1364:72751:28:27:89:526:322:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:test,  we  considered  grouping  subjects  according  to  their  CARA  midpoint  level.    These  
36:1365:72849:27:28:89:409:295:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:estimates are provided in column B and provide similar insights.   
36:1366:72916:28:28:126:528:267:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:Table  7  reveals  that  there  are  statistical  differences  in  the  overall  levels  of  
36:1367:73009:28:27:89:528:239:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:divergence  of  bids  from  risk-neutral  predictions  between  risk-averse  and  risk-neutral  
36:1368:73105:27:28:89:528:212:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:agents  that  are  consistent  with  our  theory  of  risk-averse  bidding.    However,  our  
36:1369:73199:28:27:89:528:184:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:theoretical  model  provides  an  additional  set  of  testable  implications  for  risk-averse  
36:1370:73296:27:28:89:524:157:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f4:bidding  –  these  differences  should  be  a  decreasing  function  in  observed  signals.    This 
36:1371:73395:28:28:90:527:129:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:implies  that  the  slope  of  the  bid  function  in  the  signal  space  should  be  an  increasing  
36:1372:73498:28:63:89:231:101:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:function of risk aversion.       
37:1373:73531:63:0:295:318:38:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:-36- 
37:1374:73536:0:27:126:525:708:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:To evaluate this theoretical prediction, we augment equation (17) by including an 
37:1375:73618:27:28:89:527:681:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:interaction  of  the  individual’s  risk  preference  with  his/her  induced  signal  and  signal  
37:1376:73717:28:27:89:527:653:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:squared,  and  an  interaction  of  these  values  with  the  treatment  dummies.      Empirical  
37:1377:73815:27:28:89:525:626:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:estimates from these models are contained in columns E and F in Table 6.  We obtain the 
37:1378:73903:28:28:89:266:598:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:following insight from these results: 
37:1379:73941:28:13:107:526:570:144:g_d0_f5:144:g_d0_f5:Result  6:  Risk  averse  agents  in  both  the  EA  and  OA  treatments  submit  bids  that  are  
37:1380:74040:13:14:107:527:557:144:g_d0_f5:144:g_d0_f5:conditionally  more  responsive  to  induced  signals  than  do  risk-averse  agents  in  the  
37:1381:74135:14:14:107:525:543:144:g_d0_f5:144:g_d0_f5:baseline no-resale treatment.  Furthermore, these differences decline over the range 
37:1382:74220:14:14:107:525:529:144:g_d0_f5:144:g_d0_f5:of  the  signal  space  greater  than  $20 for all but slightly risk averse agents in the EA 
37:1383:74312:14:14:107:165:515:144:g_d0_f5:144:g_d0_f5:treatment.   
37:1384:74325:14:13:107:110:501:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
37:1385:74325:13:28:89:526:488:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:The  first  part  of  Result  6  follows  from  estimated  differences  on  the  coefficients  for  the  
37:1386:74430:28:28:89:527:460:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:SRA_signal  (HRA_signal)  variable  and  the  associated  interaction  of  this  variable  with  
37:1387:74527:28:27:89:526:432:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:the  treatment  dummies.    For  example,  in  Column  E  of  Table  6  the  estimated  marginal  
37:1388:74625:27:28:89:525:405:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:effect of the induced signal on realized bids of slightly risk averse agents in the baseline 
37:1389:74718:28:27:89:529:377:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:treatment is given by [-0.325 + 0.010*signal], which  is  significant  at  the  p  <  0.05  level.    
37:1390:74820:27:28:89:528:350:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:In  contrast,  the  estimated  marginal  effect  of  the  induced  signal  on  realized  bids  for  
37:1391:74920:28:27:89:525:322:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:slightly risk averse agents in the OA resale treatment is given by [0.284 – 0.004*signal] – 
37:1392:75012:27:28:89:524:295:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:the difference in the parameter estimates for SRA_signal and SRA_OA_signal minus the 
37:1393:75097:28:29:89:527:267:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:difference  in  the  parameter  estimates  for  SRA_signal2  and  SRA_OA_signal2,  and  for  
37:1394:75190:29:28:90:524:238:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:slightly risk averse agents in the EA resale treatment the difference is given by [0.042 − 
37:1395:75280:28:28:90:174:210:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:0.001*signal].     
37:1396:75299:28:27:126:526:182:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:The  second  part  of  Result  6  follows  from  Column  F  of  Table  6,  which  provides  
37:1397:75391:27:28:89:524:155:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:parameter estimates for our bid function for all observations where the signal received by 
37:1398:75482:28:27:89:526:127:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:the  agent  was  greater  than  $20.    The  estimated  rate  of  change  in  the  slope  of  the  bid  
37:1399:75586:27:62:89:526:100:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:function  in  the  signal  space  for  slightly  risk  averse  agents  in  the  baseline  treatment  is  
38:1400:75691:62:0:295:318:38:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:-37- 
38:1401:75696:0:27:89:522:708:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:0.012.  For slightly risk averse agents in the OA resale treatment this rate of change is -
38:1402:75787:27:28:89:526:681:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:0.006 – the difference in the parameter estimates for SRA_signal2 and SRA_OA_signal2.   
38:1403:75875:28:27:90:195:653:144:g_d0_f4:144:g_d0_f4:V. Conclusions  
38:1404:75890:27:28:126:527:626:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:Auctions  are  ubiquitous.    Yet  whether  and  to  what  extent  the  introduction  of  
38:1405:75980:28:28:90:526:598:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:secondary  resale  markets  influences  bidding  behavior  when  private  values  are  uncertain  
38:1406:76078:28:27:90:525:570:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:remains largely unknown.  We begin by exploring a novel data set that provides insights 
38:1407:76166:27:28:90:525:543:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:into  the  importance  of  the  resale  effect.    Reduced-form  empirical  estimates  suggest  that  
38:1408:76268:28:27:90:525:515:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:bidding patterns are consistent with theoretical predictions.  Yet, akin to many empirical 
38:1409:76359:27:28:90:525:488:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:exercises, the strength of inference is attenuated when one considers the set of maintained 
38:1410:76451:28:28:90:467:460:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:assumptions needed to generate confident conclusions from these field data.    
38:1411:76530:28:27:126:525:432:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:Our approach to this problem is to make use of a laboratory experiment.  Such an 
38:1412:76611:27:28:90:527:405:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:effort  gives  up  much  of  the  realism  associated  with  field  data,  but  it  permits  us  to  
38:1413:76712:28:27:90:528:377:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:investigate  whether  the  resale  market  by  itself  can  lead  to  such  predicted  consequences.    
38:1414:76816:27:28:90:527:350:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:We  find  that  extant  theory  has  considerable  predictive  power,  but  the  accuracy  of  the  
38:1415:76916:28:27:90:526:322:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:theory  is  enhanced  if  we  control  for  individual  risk  preferences.    Besides  their  obvious  
38:1416:77019:27:28:90:527:295:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:importance  normatively,  these  results  have  practical  policy  significance  as  well.    For  
38:1417:77118:28:28:90:526:267:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:example,  a  necessary  condition  to  lift  the  countervailing  duty  and  anti-dumping  ruling  
38:1418:77217:28:27:90:525:239:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:against Canadian softwood lumber exporters (who export to the U.S.) is that their auction 
38:1419:77307:27:28:90:530:212:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:markets   be   robust   and   not   influenced   unduly   by   collusion.      Without   a   proper   
38:1420:77409:28:27:90:526:184:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:understanding  of  the  resale  opportunities  of  the  various  bidders,  the  modeler  may  very  
38:1421:77509:27:28:90:527:157:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:well  earmark  bidding  disparities  among  certain  bidder  types  as  evidence  of  collusion  
38:1422:77606:28:91:90:410:129:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:when it is in fact due merely to secondary market considerations.   
39:1423:77674:91:0:295:318:38:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:-38-

57:3538:105792:13:181:90:486:219:144:g_d0_f3:121:g_d0_f3:from which one obtains the claimed relationships. The proof for →∞σ is similar. 
58:3539:105871:181:0:295:318:38:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:-57- 
58:3540:105876:0:15:90:402:708:144:g_d0_f4:144:g_d0_f3:Appendix B: Experimental Instructions – OA Resale Treatment 
58:3541:105936:15:14:90:93:693:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
58:3542:105936:14:13:90:464:679:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:Welcome to Lister’s Auctions!  You have the opportunity to bid in a series of 
58:3543:106014:13:14:90:424:666:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:experimental auctions today and you can earn cash by participating.   
58:3544:106084:14:14:90:93:652:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
58:3545:106084:14:14:90:169:638:144:g_d0_f4:144:g_d0_f4:Auction Rules: 
58:3546:106099:14:14:90:514:624:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:In this auction you will bid against four (4) other people and the person with the highest 
58:3547:106190:14:13:90:510:610:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:bid is the winner, and pays the amount of their bid for the “fictitious” commodity.  The 
58:3548:106279:13:14:90:513:597:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:auction is a sealed bid auction so you don’t know the bids of the other participants.  We 
58:3549:106369:14:14:90:513:583:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:will repeat the auction for 10 rounds.  At the end of the session, your earnings from this 
58:3550:106460:14:14:90:510:569:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:experiment and another unrelated experiment will be summed and paid to you in cash.  
58:3551:106545:14:14:90:93:555:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
58:3552:106545:14:13:90:510:541:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:There are six steps in the auction process, each of which are explained in detail below.  
58:3553:106635:13:14:90:464:528:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:The six steps include: (i) determining your signal of the value of the fictitious 
58:3554:106717:14:14:90:510:514:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:commodity, (ii) determining your bid, (iii) determining your use value for the fictitious 
58:3555:106807:14:14:90:490:500:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:good, (iv) determining the winner, (v) the resale market, and (vi) determining your 
58:3556:106891:14:14:90:199:486:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:payouts for the round. 
58:3557:106914:14:13:90:93:472:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
58:3558:106914:13:14:108:523:459:144:g_d0_f4:144:g_d0_f3:1.  Determining your signal of the good’s value:  At the beginning of each period, a 
58:3559:106999:14:14:108:522:445:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:monitor will hand you a card numbered from zero dollars ($0) to fifty dollars ($50) in 
58:3560:107086:14:14:108:511:431:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:one dollar ($1) increments.  The value on the card handed to you will be a signal of 
58:3561:107171:14:14:108:504:417:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:your use value for the fictitious good.  The other bidders in your auction will have 
58:3562:107256:14:13:108:524:403:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:their signals determined in exactly the same way.  Signals are private and independent 
58:3563:107343:13:14:108:391:390:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:across buyers, and your signal will change across rounds.   
58:3564:107403:14:14:108:111:376:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
58:3565:107403:14:14:126:243:362:144:g_d0_f5:144:g_d0_f5:Signals and Use Values 
58:3566:107426:14:14:126:129:348:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
58:3567:107426:14:13:126:525:334:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:Use values, V, in each round are drawn from a uniform distribution on the interval 
58:3568:107509:13:14:126:500:321:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:[10, 40].  That is, every dollar value between 10 and 40 is equally likely to be 
58:3569:107590:14:14:126:517:307:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:drawn as your use value.  These values are independently drawn for each subject 
58:3570:107670:14:14:126:272:293:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:and will differ across periods. 
58:3571:107702:14:14:126:129:279:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
58:3572:107702:14:13:126:514:265:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:The signal you will receive is determined by adding a random number drawn on 
58:3573:107779:13:14:126:522:252:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:the interval [-10, 10] to your use value.  Again, each dollar value between -10 and 
58:3574:107863:14:14:126:502:238:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:10 is equally likely to be drawn and added to your use value.  Your first-stage 
58:3575:107943:14:14:126:263:224:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:signal, S, is hence given by: 
58:3576:107973:14:13:126:129:210:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
58:3577:107973:13:15:345:387:197:142:g_d0_f5:144:g_d0_f3:numberrandomVS += 
58:3578:107989:15:13:126:129:182:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
58:3579:107989:13:14:126:417:169:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:Your signal, S, is thus distributed on the interval [$0, $50].   
58:3580:108054:14:14:126:129:155:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
58:3581:108054:14:14:126:518:141:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:Given your signal, you can compute the expected use value.  For example, if you 
58:3582:108134:14:14:126:500:127:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:were to receive a signal of $30 in the first stage, you know that your final use 
58:3583:108215:14:13:126:522:113:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:value must lie somewhere in the interval [$20, $40].  Since each of these values is 
58:3584:108299:13:62:126:516:100:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:equally likely to have been selected as your use value, on average your use value 
59:3585:108381:62:0:295:318:38:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:-58- 
59:3586:108386:0:13:126:508:708:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:is $30.  However, any value in this range could have been assigned as your use 
59:3587:108465:13:14:126:164:695:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:value.   
59:3588:108474:14:14:108:111:681:144:g_d0_f4:144:g_d0_f4: 
59:3589:108474:14:14:108:514:667:144:g_d0_f4:144:g_d0_f3:2.  Determining your bid value:  After receiving your signal, you will choose your 
59:3590:108557:14:14:108:497:653:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:bid value for the fictitious good.  In order to choose your bid, consider how your 
59:3591:108640:14:13:108:523:639:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:earnings for each period are calculated.  If you are the person with the highest bid you 
59:3592:108729:13:14:108:515:626:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:are the winner of the auction.  Your earnings are equal to your use value minus your 
59:3593:108814:14:14:108:349:612:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:bid amount if you have the highest end use value: 
59:3594:108864:14:14:108:111:598:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
59:3595:108864:14:14:192:440:584:144:g_d0_f4:144:g_d0_f4:Earnings = your good’s use value (V) – your bid 
59:3596:108912:14:13:315:318:570:144:g_d0_f4:144:g_d0_f4: 
59:3597:108912:13:14:108:516:557:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:If you are the person with the highest bid but do not have the highest use value, your 
59:3598:108999:14:14:108:518:543:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:earnings are equal to the highest use value of all participants minus your bid amount: 
59:3599:109086:14:14:108:111:529:144:g_d0_f4:144:g_d0_f4: 
59:3600:109086:14:14:214:419:515:144:g_d0_f4:144:g_d0_f4:Earnings = highest use value – your bid 
59:3601:109126:14:13:108:111:501:144:g_d0_f4:144:g_d0_f4: 
59:3602:109126:13:14:108:501:488:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:If you are not the high bidder in a round, your earnings for the period are zero.  If 
59:3603:109212:14:14:107:503:474:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:there is a tie, the winner will be determined by the flip of a coin (if more than two 
59:3604:109298:14:14:107:521:460:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:people tie we will draw a card to determine the winner).  Your bid can be any amount 
59:3605:109383:14:14:107:498:446:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:in the range from zero ($0) to forty dollars ($40) in ten cent ($0.10) increments.   
59:3606:109468:14:13:107:110:432:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
59:3607:109468:13:14:108:509:419:144:g_d0_f4:144:g_d0_f3:3.  Determining your use value:  Once all bids have been received, a monitor will 
59:3608:109550:14:14:108:496:405:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:hand you a second slip of paper numbered from ten dollars ($10) to forty dollars 
59:3609:109631:14:14:108:519:391:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:($40) that gives your final use value, V.  Your use value will lie within 10$±of your 
59:3610:109717:14:14:108:161:377:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:signal, S.   
59:3611:109730:14:14:108:111:363:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
59:3612:109730:14:14:108:491:349:144:g_d0_f4:144:g_d0_f3:4.  Determining the auction winner:  All bids will be publicly announced and 
59:3613:109807:14:13:108:509:335:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:recorded by a monitor on the blackboard.  Your bid will be compared with those of 
59:3614:109889:13:14:108:513:322:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:the four other participants in the auction.  The person with the highest bid amount is 
59:3615:109976:14:14:108:165:308:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:the winner. 
59:3616:109988:14:14:108:111:294:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
59:3617:109988:14:14:108:511:280:144:g_d0_f4:144:g_d0_f3:5.  The resale market: In the resale market, each participant can see the use values 
59:3618:110073:14:13:108:488:266:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:for all other participants.  The highest bidder in the auction market will sell the 
59:3619:110157:13:14:108:470:253:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:“fictitious” commodity to the individual with the highest use value.  In this 
59:3620:110235:14:14:108:514:239:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:experiment this happens automatically.  The payoff for the winner is the highest use 
59:3621:110320:14:14:108:503:225:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:value of all participants minus his/her bid amount.  If you did not win the auction, 
59:3622:110405:14:14:108:503:211:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:your payout for the period will be zero.  The payout for the auction winner can be 
59:3623:110488:14:13:108:401:197:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:positive even if your bid was greater than your use value.      
59:3624:110552:13:14:108:111:184:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
59:3625:110552:14:14:108:510:170:144:g_d0_f4:144:g_d0_f3:6.  Determining your payouts:  If you are the auction winner, you will receive the 
59:3626:110635:14:14:108:524:156:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:difference between the highest use value and your bid.  If you did not win the auction, 
59:3627:110723:14:14:108:522:142:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:you receive zero for that period.  Your total earnings for this experiment is the sum of 
59:3628:110812:14:13:108:312:128:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:your earnings for each of the 10 periods.   
59:3629:110856:13:14:90:93:115:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
59:3630:110856:14:63:90:358:101:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:Do you have any questions about the auction process?   
60:3631:110911:63:0:295:318:38:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:-59- 
60:3632:110916:0:15:90:434:708:144:g_d0_f4:144:g_d0_f3:Appendix C: Experimental Instructions for Risk Aversion Experiment 
60:3633:110983:15:14:90:93:693:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
60:3634:110983:14:13:125:516:679:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: Record your subject number from the previous part on your decision sheet. Your 
60:3635:111062:13:14:89:502:666:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:decision sheet shows ten decisions listed on the left.  Each decision is a paired choice 
60:3636:111151:14:14:89:518:652:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:between OPTION A and OPTION B.  You will make ten choices and record these in the 
60:3637:111233:14:14:89:509:638:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:final column, but only one of them will be used in the end to determine your earnings.  
60:3638:111321:14:14:89:509:624:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:Before you start making your ten choices, please let me explain how these choices will 
60:3639:111408:14:13:89:338:610:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:affect your earnings for this part of the experiment. 
60:3640:111462:13:14:89:92:597:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
60:3641:111462:14:14:125:515:583:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: We will use part of a deck of cards to determine payoffs; cards 2-10 and the Ace 
60:3642:111543:14:14:89:509:569:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:will represent “1”.  After you have made all of your choices, we will randomly select a 
60:3643:111631:14:14:89:486:555:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:card twice, once to select one of the ten decisions to be used, and a second time to 
60:3644:111716:14:13:90:482:541:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:determine what your payoff is for the option you chose, A or B, for the particular 
60:3645:111799:13:14:90:515:528:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:decision selected. (After the first card is selected, it will be put back in the pile, the deck 
60:3646:111895:14:14:90:511:514:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:will be reshuffled, and the second card will be drawn.)  Even though you will make ten 
60:3647:111982:14:14:90:509:500:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:decisions, only one of these will end up affecting your earnings, but you will not know 
60:3648:112070:14:14:90:510:486:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:in advance which decision will be used.  Obviously, each decision has an equal chance 
60:3649:112156:14:13:90:211:472:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:of being used in the end. 
60:3650:112182:13:14:90:93:459:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
60:3651:112182:14:14:125:507:445:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: Now, please look at Decision 1 at the top.  OPTION A pays $2.00 if the Ace is 
60:3652:112260:14:14:90:502:431:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:selected, and it pays $1.60 if the card selected is 2-10.  OPTION B yields $3.85 if the 
60:3653:112348:14:14:90:502:417:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:Ace is selected, and it pays $0.10 if the card selected is 2-10.  The other decisions are 
60:3654:112438:14:13:90:499:403:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:similar, except that as you move down the table, the chances of the higher payoff for 
60:3655:112524:13:14:90:503:390:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:each option increase.  In fact, for Decision 10 in the bottom row, the cards will not be 
60:3656:112613:14:14:90:478:376:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:needed since each option pays the highest payoff for sure, so your choice here is 
60:3657:112695:14:14:90:209:362:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:between $2.00 or $3.85. 
60:3658:112719:14:14:90:93:348:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
60:3659:112719:14:13:125:507:334:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: To summarize, you will make ten choices: for each decision row you will have 
60:3660:112796:13:14:90:507:321:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:to choose between OPTION A and OPTION B.  You may choose A for some decision 
60:3661:112873:14:14:90:505:307:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:rows and B for other rows, and you may change your decisions and make them in any 
60:3662:112955:14:14:90:508:293:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:order.  When you are finished, we will come to your desk and pick a card to determine 
60:3663:113041:14:14:90:495:279:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:which of the ten decisions will be used.  Then we will put the card back in the deck, 
60:3664:113127:14:13:90:511:265:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:shuffle, and select a card again to determine your money earnings for the OPTION you 
60:3665:113212:13:14:90:474:252:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:chose for that decision.  Earnings for this choice will be added to your previous 
60:3666:113294:14:14:90:412:238:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:earnings, and you will be paid all earnings in cash when we finish. 
60:3667:113362:14:14:90:93:224:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
60:3668:113362:14:14:126:518:210:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: So now please look at the empty boxes on the right side of the record sheet.  You 
60:3669:113444:14:13:90:509:196:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:will have to write a decision, A or B in each of these boxes, and then the card selection 
60:3670:113534:13:14:90:513:183:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:will determine which one is going to count.  We will look at the decision that you made 
60:3671:113622:14:14:90:508:169:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:for the choice that counts, and circle it, before selecting a card again to determine your 
60:3672:113713:14:14:90:504:155:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:earnings for this part.  Then you will write your earnings in the blank at the bottom of 
60:3673:113802:14:14:90:136:141:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:the page. 
60:3674:113812:14:13:90:93:127:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: 
60:3675:113812:13:14:126:508:114:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3: Are there any questions?  Now you may begin making your choices.  Please do 
60:3676:113888:14:14:90:473:100:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:not talk with anyone else while we are doing this; raise your hand if you have a 
60:3677:113969:14:0:90:137:86:144:g_d0_f3:144:g_d0_f3:question.
